           <div class="_8sz1 _8sz5 _8szd _8szj" id="u_0_11">
            <div class="_8t03 _8tm_">
             <a class="_8ulx" href="/groups/451831955405722/">
              <div class="_8uly">
               <div class="_8wo2"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 美國減醣減脂-輕鬆瘦
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 減醣、減脂、減肥、就是不減健康！讓我們用美國當地可以買到的食材來達到減醣飲食，用美國當地最方便的方式來達到瘦身的效果。 "心"如果沒有改變、體重就不會改變。一定先要"有心"才能改變體重。改變體重不光光是為了自己變好看變健康、更是為了你愛的人。今天的體重是日積月累的飲食及生活型態的"結果"，如果要改變現在的體重，就一定不能再用以前的吃法跟發胖的生活作息。"有心"的人找到入口、"沒有心"的人找到藉口! 就從今天開始"擇食" "有氧" 養成"易瘦體質"! 減肥第一重點就"吃"，其實醣減下來其實就自然而然地瘦了，只要吃的正確不用挨餓也能飽飽地瘦身。減醣一點都不難，只要你對食物有正確的認識就不會吃錯。選擇低醣飲食，直直瘦就是必然發生的結果。 減重不等於減肥，要消滅的是危害身體的"脂肪"而不是肌肉。看到體重數字減少的時候不要開心地太早，先減掉的一定是水分，如果方法錯誤再來減掉的就是肌肉。想呼吸睡覺都瘦就得靠肌肉，肌肉是幫助我們燃燒脂肪的大功臣，減掉肌肉絕對是大忌。有些人減肥會越減越肥，就是吃錯食物用錯方法導致減去肌肉留了一身肥油還沾沾自喜以為減"肥"成功。所以一定要用對的方法減肥，而不是光追求減"重"這件事。 減肥是一種生活態度，唯有不反彈的瘦身才是王道。吃對食物、用對方法、找一個自己能接受且能持續的方式才會越吃越瘦、越來越健康! 免責聲明：管理員團隊不是醫生，這裡所分享的知識，來自於學到的各科通識教育，以及本身的經驗。每個人身體狀況不同，任何健康飲食方式的改變，在執行之前都應該先諮詢專業的保健醫生。對於本團任何資料或建議所引致的損失或傷害，管理員團隊和本社團毋須承擔任何責任。
                </div>
               </div>

                 南加州母乳媽媽加油團Chinese-speaking Breastfeeding Support Group
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 每位母乳媽媽都需要無上限的精神支持!歡迎各位住在美國的母乳媽媽一起來分享母乳哺餵的甘苦談，一起堅持努力給寶寶最珍貴的營養與健康! 我本身是美國認證的泌乳諮詢師/拉梅茲生產講師/認證陪產士(分娩導樂)/產後照護士(產後導樂)，也是兩個寶的媽。設立這個社團的目的，是希望在美國的母乳媽媽們能有一個安全健康的交流平台。我期許這裡沒有批評與苛責，只有鼓勵與安慰。不論你有哺乳問題想要發問、或是餵/擠奶累了想討抱、或是可愛的母奶寶寶炫耀文，歡迎你隨時發聲！如果妳需要LC協助，我有提供到府泌乳諮詢&amp;輔導(in-home visit lactation counseling)，大部分PPO保險計劃都有給付，有需要的媽咪可以私訊我，或參考我的網站：themamamoon.com

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Spirituality &amp; Meditation
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Spirituality, in a narrow sense, concerns itself with matters of the spirit. The spiritual, involving (as it may) perceived eternal verities regarding humankind's ultimate nature, often contrasts with the temporal, with the material, or with the worldly. A sense of connection forms a central defining characteristic of spirituality — connection to something greater than oneself, which includes an emotional experience of religious awe and reverence. Equally importantly, spirituality relates to matters of sanity and of psychological health. Like some forms of religion, spirituality often focuses on personal experience. Spirituality may involve perceiving life as higher, more complex or more integrated with one's worldview, as contrasted with the merely sensual. The term Meditation describes a variety of practices with a variety of goals. It usually involves turning our attention inward to the mind itself. Meditation is often recognized as a component of Eastern religions, having originated Vedic Hinduism. It has also become mainstream in Western culture. It encompasses any of a wide variety of spiritual practices which emphasize mental activity or quiescence. Meditation can also be used for personal development, such as the exercises of Hatha yoga. Many practice meditation in order to achieve eternal peace, while others do it in order to become healthier.
                </div>
               </div>
               <div>
                <div class="_8um4">
                 <span class="_8ul_"><i class="_8wo5 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_8f3bf5"></i><span class="_8um1">4.4&nbsp;万位成员</span></span><span class="_8um0"><i class="_8wo6 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_ce40e2"></i><span class="_8um2">0 篇新帖</span></span>

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Applied Behavior Analysis
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This closed group is a private forum exclusively for ABA Professionals actively certified and registered in good standing by the Behaviour Analyst Certification Board (BACB) to promote the science and dissemination of Applied Behaviour Analysis. The rules outlined below are non-negotiable. All membership requests are reviewed by group administrators. Professionals of related disciplines will be accepted at the discretion of the group administrators. We acknowledge each other as equals with respect to ability, age, appearance, class, ethnicity, gender, neurotype, religion, sex, sexual orientation, and other identity groups. We provide useful comments, affirmative to the principles of ABA, and respectful when in disagreement. Criticisms and negative experiences of ABA should be worded in a professional and respectful manner. We expect that what is said here, stays here (distribution of screenshots of group conversations will result in removal from the group). Posts can be saved for future reference by clicking the three dots at the top right of the post and selecting “save post.” We base our discussions on the science, principles, and ethics of Applied Behaviour Analysis and the Behaviour Analyst Certification Board (BACB). Discussions will focus on evidence-based therapies, applications, treatments, and interventions. •Any and all comments and posts are reviewed by the group administrators and can be deleted at administrator discretion. Posts that will be deleted immediately include extremist, derogatory, libelous, factually inaccurate, and/or slanderous behaviour and/or verbiage. Any and all comments/posts must align with the BACB’s Professional and Ethical Compliance Code (PECC). •Personal attacks directed at members of the group, including group administrators, will not be tolerated. Members are expected to engage with one another and group administrators respectfully; refraining from name-calling and foul language. The offending member can be removed immediately without notice. •Business solicitations and CEU offerings are not permitted outside of weekly designated threads. Product, service, and job opportunity posts are not allowed. •Repeated posts and comments (spam) are not allowed and will be removed. •If a member is unsure if their desired post will violate any of the group rules, they are encouraged to send a private message to group administrators. •If a member would like to report or discuss a member, post, or any other matter they are encouraged to send a private message to the group administrators. *Members may not block group administrators. 
                </div>
               </div>
               <div>
                <div class="_8um4">

                 Uterine Fibroid Support &amp; Resource Group
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 PLEASE ANSWER THE QUESTIONS THAT WILL POP UP WHEN YOU REQUEST TO JOIN THE GROUP. PLEASE ALSO READ THE PINNED POST (rules) as soon as your membership is approved! - Da This is a support and resource group for all women (and trans men) to learn about the symptoms, possible causes of, treatments for and to share their experiences with uterine fibroids. It is estimated that 20-80% of women develop uterine fibroids by age 50. Fibroids are muscular tumors that grow in the wall of the uterus (womb). Fibroids are almost always benign (not cancerous). More information can be found in the links and articles that will be posted in this group. Please invite all of your lady friends to join. Thanks to all who post and share their experiences, I hoped that this page would provide a place to do just that, and it makes me so happy :) McKenzie

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 STOP BULLIES AND SUICIDE (Re-Opened)
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 ━━━━━━━━━━━ ●●● ABOUT US ●●● * Welcome to Stop Bullies &amp; Suicide ©, "SBS" for short. We are a support group to learn, share, and raise awareness about the affects that bullying and suicide have on people as well as the causes that lead up to sudden bullying and or suicide. Whether you are struggling with addiction, suicidal tenancies, depression, post-traumatic stress, or even hate crimes, we are all struggling with something - and that is why we are here - to support one another and to let people know they are not alone and they can succeed in life and to let people know that they are stronger than people deem them as. Just that one second hug or a one minute talk can change someones perspective on life or even their emotion. We welcome and support anyone and everyone, no matter your background, sexuality, race, disability, age, etc. Be the helping hand and lend an ear, one life saved is better than one life lost, and if we can continue to support others and be kind to others - we can make change happen. ━━━━━━━━━━━ ●●● HOW DID THIS GROUP START ●●● This group started in 2013, shortly after I (Michael Cary) lost my grandmother to suicide on December 5, 2012. In memory of her, I took a stance against suicide and made a promise to myself to do the best I could to help others. In addition, after being bullied my entire life for the smallest things such as for the things I liked, to the large things such as how I look or how much I weighed - it impacted me further to take a stance against bullying. No one should have to face these issues alone, and luckily I did not as I had the help from my family. ━━━━━━━━━━━ ●●● DISCLAIMERS ●●● * Stop Bullies &amp; Suicide © is solely an online support group and not affiliated with any other support groups, government agencies, or prevention organizations. * Stop Bullies &amp; Suicide © is not responsible for any actions taken upon your account such as but not limited to; Facebook ban, Facebook suspension, group ban, group removal, group mute, post deletion, or comment deletion. * Stop Bullies &amp; Suicide © is not legally responsible or liable for the advice or support that is received. Any recommendation or other information within the forum which is followed by you is at your own risk. * Stop Bullies &amp; Suicide © is subject to Copyright Protection, including all official logos and products. * Stop Bullies &amp; Suicide © has a right to refuse membership to anyone. * Stop Bullies &amp; Suicide © is not responsible or liable for contacts via messaging, calling, video calling, emailing, commenting, etc unless they are in or within our support group.
                </div>

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Healthy Meal Prep
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Healthy eating means eating a variety of foods that give you the nutrients you need to maintain your health, feel good, and have energy. These nutrients include protein, carbohydrates, fat, water, vitamins, and minerals. Nutrition is important for everyone. When combined with being physically active and maintaining a healthy weight, eating well is an excellent way to help your body stay strong and healthy. If you have a history of breast cancer or are currently undergoing treatment, eating well is especially important for you. What you eat can affect your immune system, your mood, and your energy level. No food or diet can prevent you from getting breast cancer. While researchers are still studying the effects of eating unhealthy food on breast cancer and recurrence risk, we do know that being overweight is a risk factor for both first-time and recurrent breast cancer. In this section, you can learn how to eat in a way that keeps your body as healthy as it can be. Healthy eating is not about strict dietary limitations, staying unrealistically thin, or depriving yourself of the foods you love. Rather, it’s about feeling great, having more energy, improving your health, and boosting your mood. If you feel overwhelmed by all the conflicting nutrition and diet advice out there, you’re not alone. It seems that for every expert who tells you a certain food is good for you, you’ll find another saying exactly the opposite. But by using these simple tips, you can cut through the confusion and learn how to create and stick to a tasty, varied, and nutritious diet that is as good for your mind as it is for your body. What is a healthy diet? Eating a healthy diet doesn’t have to be overly complicated. While some specific foods or nutrients have been shown to have a beneficial effect on mood, it’s your overall dietary pattern that is most important. The cornerstone of a healthy diet pattern should be to replace processed food with real food whenever possible. Eating food that is as close as possible to the way nature made it can make a huge difference to the way you think, look, and feel.
                </div>
               </div>

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Disability Support and Self-advocacy in HUD, Section 8 &amp; Low-Income Housing
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Important: To join this group you must ANSWER THE SCREENING QUESTIONS! We are having a problem with people not answering the screening the questions. If you cannot see the screening questions, please send a message to an admin. Thank you. We are looking forward to hearing from you. This group provides support and information for people with disabilities, family members of people with disabilities, and caregivers. You must be either living in, applying for, or interested in applying for a HUD funded housing program. You do NOT need to be disabled by Social security standards. You do NOT need to be receiving disability. We welcome anyone who considers themselves a person with disabilities. We also welcome you if you are a household member of a person with disabilities or if anyone under your care considers themselves a person with a disability. The group focuses on low income housing programs - primarily Section 8 and Public Housing. We also welcome discussions of other programs, such as LIHTC, 811, 202 and homeownership programs. If you feel you should join the group and do not fall into the above criteria, please let us know your reason for wishing to join.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Transcendental Meditation
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 The Transcendental Meditation® (TM®) program of Maharishi Mahesh Yogi is the single most effective meditation technique available to gain deep relaxation, eliminate stress, promote good health, increase creativity and intelligence, and attain inner happiness and fulfillment. More than six million people of all ages, educational backgrounds, cultures and religions have learned the Transcendental Meditation technique. The benefits of the Transcendental Meditation program have been verified by over 600 scientific studies at more than 200 independent research institutions in 35 countries. The Transcendental Meditation technique is easy to learn, enjoyable to practice, and enriches all areas of life. The Transcendental Meditation technique is a simple, natural, effortless procedure practiced 20 minutes twice a day, sitting comfortably with the eyes closed. This practical, proven meditation procedure requires no effort or concentration, no special skills, and no change of lifestyle. The Transcendental Meditation technique must be learned personally from a certified teacher of the Transcendental Meditation program. The technique cannot be learned from a book, video or audio tape. The purpose of the group is to bring together at one platform the practitioners, teachers, students and people who want to learn the technique so that the benefits of the technique can be shared by everyone. All are cordially invited to contribute to the group their knowledge and resources about Transcendental Meditation.

                 Keto Recipes for Beginners is a group for those interested in learning to cook for the Ketogenic Diet. We call it a diet but it is a WOE - way of eating for life. Together, we will become experts in Cooking and living KETO. You can get daily recipes at https://completelyketo.com or via Facebook messenger at https:/m.me/completelyketo WE WANT YOUR RECIPES, HOWEVER, please check your recipe ingredients. If all ingredients are not Keto friendly, recipe will be DELETED. If you post a product and an admin or moderator tells you it's not Keto do not argue with them. It will lead to an immediate ban. Similarly the answer of "but it works for me" is not acceptable. This is a zero spam or selling zone for members. Please do not post links to your own blogs or other Facebook groups. We DO NOT use or support Exogenous Ketone products. PLEASE DO NOT post or try to sell or encourage these products. You will be banned IMMEDIATELY from the site. We just don't think they are healthy. THESE ARE THE RULES FOR OUR GROUP. 1. USE THE SEARCH FUNCTION to the left of the posts. Common questions and concerns may already have been discussed at length. We won't accept posts that you can find the answer with a simple search. 2. Please do not post ANY articles or links. There is so much mis-information out there we just delete them. 3. Please do not post links other websites. We delete them because we do not have the time to check each link. 4. Please be kind. Rudeness won't be tolerated. Foul language, bullying or bashing of others will get you banned. 5. Cheat posts of any kind will be deleted and you will be banned. Take responsibility for what you eat. If you cheat, move forward without posting about it.. 6. Please DO post recipes. Make sure they are 100% Keto friendly before posting. Do NOT post Non-keto recipes with suggested substitutions. Non-keto recipes will be deleted. We do not accept video recipes or Facebook live videos. 7. IF YOU ARE BEING PRIVATELY MESSAGED, offering to sell you something, block them and LET US KNOW. 8. To follow a post please go up to the right side of the post and click the three dots and select get notifications. Do not type F, following a . or anything similar. You will be muted and unable to comment for 24 hours. 9. Our admins and moderators are here to help you. Arguing with them, disrespecting them, referring to them as "Keto police" or "Keto Nazis" will result in an immediate removal from the group. 10. From time to time, Admin, may post links to products we think are of value. You may assume that some of these links are affiliate links. We only recommend products we believe in. We are a participant in the Amazon Services LLC Associates Program, an affiliate advertising program designed to provide a means for us to earn fees by linking to Amazon.com and affiliated sites. Learn, share, and grow, and lets SHARE RECIPES.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Lefora Filipino Nurses To US
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Lefora Filipino Nurses to US is a Facebook Page made up of over 80,000+ members and growing with more individuals, particularly Filipino nurses, joining the group every day. These nurses have the same goal — to be granted EB3 VISAs so that they may be able to work in the United States. Some also aim to be granted migration VISAs so that they can be with their spouses and children when they finally get the chance to work abroad. The process is not easy and some had to wait for years before getting their application approved. Some have been denied several times despite being highly qualified yet they continue to apply and wish for the best. Lefora Filipino Nurses to US is a hub where these nurses who have a similar goal get together so that their stories and information can be shared with each other. Anyone in the group can post a question anytime if they are confused about a certain procedure and others simply share their story with hopes that it may inspire or even help those who are still in the process of applying for a VISA.

                 High Vibes
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 The posts I share in this group are a reflection of my inner transformation. When I share a post, I never mean to tell anyone what to do or think. My posts are meant to be thought-provoking because that is what they are to me. Every single message that I have posted in the last 6 years since High Vibes was started has been a reflection of myself and my journey of growth. I started this group because I thought there might be other people out there who are going through the same things I am. I understand that not everyone in this world is going to identify with my thoughts, and that's okay with me. Just as I send blessings to those who do not share my way of thinking, I hope that others will do the same for me. Namaste &lt;3 The purpose of this group is to serve as an inspiration and discussion platform to talk about the ways in which subtle energy balance, yoga, meditation, and spirituality affect our life. Our energy centers (chakras) reflect our current energetic state and influence our aura. A balanced chakra system allows for a smooth flow of energy within and around the body. Meditation is beneficial to our physical, mental, emotional, and spiritual bodies. It is also a very effective tool for tapping into your true self and developing your intuitive abilities. All members are welcome to post messages relating to energy balance, yoga, meditation, and spirituality. If messages do not relate to the true essence of High Vibes, please understand that they will not be posted. We want to keep the vibes pure. Please do not abuse this platform for commercial purposes or for political messages. Videos of a person/people talking will not be posted, as such videos tend to focus a great deal on the speaker(s) and not so much on the message. If you have something to say, please write it in a post. As the administrator, I cannot spend 20 minutes watching a video to see if it fits in with High Vibes' philosophy. Thanks for understanding! Please remember to be kind when you post something or reply to a post. High Vibes reserves the right to delete any unkind comments. Brightest Blessings &lt;3 Erika Marie Rose

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Anxiety Stress &amp; Panic Attack Support
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Here we discuss topics related to Heath Anxiety, General Anxiety, Panic Disorder, Depression &amp; Stress, Addiction, and self-improvement! I will post my YouTube channel "Trey Jones" uploads on here after posting them to YouTube. If you have not Subscribed to the YouTube channel, I encourage you to do so! Created this group to have a forum type setting where we can discuss all of the topics listed above! There will be NO Excessive Profanity, NO Spamming, NO Putting Others Down. I encourage EVERYONE to Add FB friends to this group who you believe could benefit from the topics discussed! GROUP RULES (MUST READ) 1.) There will be No Harrassing or Bullying other members. This will result in you being blocked from the group! If this is happening to you or others, please report it! 2.) No Excessive Profanity. ZERO F BOMBS or inappropriate sexual comments. You guys know what Excessive means I'm sure. Admins &amp; Moderators will be the judge of excessive. No sexual comments. This isn't a dating site. 3.) Flirt at your own risk! If someone takes offense and reports you for inappropriate behavior then you will be gone if I agree with the claim. No asking for only the opposite sex to message you! 4.) No Self Promotion. Yes I promote my videos, but this group was meant to be an extention of my Youtube channel community. I cant automatically trust every person who comes into the group and the first post is to sell their book, product, website or blog. I dont have time to always review certain links, but you are welcome to send them to me to review. If I dont get back to you, no hard feelings. 5.) No Heart Rate or Blood Pressure App Screen shots or pics. These apps only hold people back from recovery and can be possible triggers. 6.) No "Im Dying Posts" "Suicidal Posts" or "Cutting Posts." The admins and mods have a protocol for this. Send the suicide hotline, contact a family member, turn on post approval and remove the post. Its important to seek help, but do so without jeapordizing and triggering the entire group. 7.) PLEASE Label Distraction Posts “Distraction Post” Some subjects are too off topic to be acceptable regardless of the label. Distraction Posts should be positive and help those with anxiety focus on something else. A random selfie, drama, or asking for gaming info is not acceptable. 8.) Live videos 30 min or less &amp; 1 every 3 days! (Excluding admins &amp; moderators) They are to be only beneficial to the group. No self promotion, sexual, selling, cutting, suicidal activity or unrelated material allowed. Lives are for those trying to help or spread a positive message. Keep them positive. 9.) Unrelated Posts is a very broad term and posts and severity ranging from warnings to blocking will applied. Yes some posts that are labeled distraction posts will be fine, but that is for the admins and moderators to decide. No drama posts or excessive selfies without a message. 10.) No posts asking for diagnosis! Seek professionals over peers!

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Cerebral Palsy PARENTS information group
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group has been created as we want it to be a parent based group of families with cerbral palsy in their lives. Whether it's family, children, friends, please feel free to join to support eachother with converstation around therapy, and succeess, and opportunities! Welcome to the Cerebral Palsy PARENTS Information Group! This group is meant to be a community where PARENTS of children who have cerebral palsy can discuss issues, celebrate successes and ask questions related to our children and their specific needs. There have been quite a few posts that are "sales" in nature recently. Those will no longer be permitted and will be deleted. If you notice members doing so --- whether selling products or treatments --- please message the Admins. We have families and can't be on the page all the time. We will need everyone's help to keep the content what it is meant to be --- a supportive community where PARENTS of children who have cp can discuss issues related to our children. On the note of being SUPPORTIVE, one of the reasons this group was created was due to "bad behavior" of folks in other similar groups. We don't all have to agree on every issue, but we must be respectful and supportive here. Any behavior that is rude to others will get the person banned from the group. Re: Fundraising posts: Unfortunately, fundraising is something that is necessary for most, if not all of us, to meet our children's needs. That said, we do not want this group content to be just a collection of fundraising posts. We are asking for NO fundraising posts. If you are choosing to hope to join this group to gain access to more people for fundraising opportunities. Please graciously don't ask to join. We as admins have also decided not to have "shares" or links, Facebook pages, or really anything as we are trying to keep the feed relevant to conversation and support. The amount of sharing that we see in our own personal feeds and other groups, we feel that we don't want the feeds clogged losing pertinent questions or conversations through the feeds. Thank you all for being here and for being respectful of these rules. We appreciate your posts and comments about your children very much, as well as your help to others regarding figuring out ways to better help their children.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Disability Awareness Advocacy Group
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is an advocacy group, that advocates for the disabled community. Question; Are you a coach of a sports facility? Are you an advocate for an organization? or an community group? Are you a teacher looking for a group that will encourage your school class? Are you a parent or an care giver who is concerned about your love one? Now we have a group of parents who can help. At this time we we don't have a meeting date yet for our parents. We will soon. Please check this group for more updates. We can help, we have knowledgeable people who has been or educating the public about the issues facing the disabled community around the world. For example members has been advocating for human rights, education, employment, access and recreation. For some time now members have been subporting each other in a variety of ways. For example having online meetings, surveys,, and information sessions Our mission is to empower individuals with disabilities, to get involved in what the city has to offer, and to be creative in creating their own projects, groups, and whatever else they decide to do as a career. Now if you check out this group, most members do have there own community groups focussing on these issues. For example access, transportation, health, and housing. We do have focuss groups that looks in to these issues. Don't miss out in the fun. Join our online radio show on spreaker today. You will hear music, talk shows,, and so much more. Please go to www.spreaker.com or e-mail me at leon.wilson.1401@facebook.com Members of disability awareness advocacy group can be mentors to the disabled community. Keep in mind,when you join the disability awareness advocacy group, you will have an important role, that is to support the disabled community as much as you can by spreading the word about the group, and by organizing community events that promotes accessibility and inclusion in a fun way. Group policies; The group's policy on membership is simple as this, members are expected to participate, and share there interests of topics that interests them and report on any wrong doing by members of Disability Awareness Advocacy Group. Policy on commitment; Members of Disability Awareness Advocacy Group, remember it's about empowering you to seek out individuals and form your own group and become an advocate for peoples with disabilituies. For guidance check out the website. START THE MOVEMENT WHERE YOU LIVE! A message from Leon Your disability awareness campaign manager/mentor.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Fertility Awareness Method of Birth Control
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 **You MUST answer the admission questions to be accepted into the group. If you cannot see these questions when you request to join, please PM our associated page - bit.ly/FAM-Page** This group is a safe, non-judging, women-only group for any woman who practices the Fertility Awareness Method, which consists of observing your fertility signs - Body Basal Temperature, Cervical Mucus, and/or Cervix position - to track your fertility for conception, avoiding pregnancy, or health reasons. You're welcome to join; it doesn't matter which fertility awareness method (FAM) you use, although be aware that this group's primary focus is the Sympto-Thermal Method (Cervical Fluid &amp; Basal Body Temperature) as one of the most highly effective methods available. This means that we DO NOT advocate the use of the rhythm/calendar method nor the "fertility apps/devices" which utilize only basal body temperature to compute fertility with proprietary algorithms (eg Natural Cycles, Daysy, LadyComp, Ava). If you are seriously interested in learning FAM, you're also welcome to join. We will help you during the learning process. Shared accounts where there's a male involved are not accepted, sorry - it is of utmost importance to us to keep our promise of women-only at this time. More insight into the method can be found in this incredible book: amzn.to/2mkQGGI Please visit our website for LOTS of resources - most of our group files are being moved to the website - please be patient as we continue to develop and improve our website - https://fertilityawarenessmethodofbirthcontrol.com/ By requesting membership to this group and making a post, you are deemed to have read and agreed to the group's Community Guidelines, read the Getting Started file, and reviewed the group UNITS. Fertility awareness is not conservative. It's not liberal, hippie-ish, or Christian. It's not exclusively for environmentalists or vegans, Catholics or Muslims, the rich or the poor. Fertility Awareness is an essentially human project by which a woman learns to interpret the signs her body gives that indicate her fertility. It is therefore a form of self-knowledge that empowers couples to achieve or avoid pregnancy without reliance on artificial technology. It enables women to recognize any reproductive health issues they may have. It is a deep respect for the human body, and as such, it is for all women, everywhere.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 ANXIETY/PANIC ATTACKS LETS FIND A CURE!!!
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                  Member Guidelines Please Read before your initial post Guidelines for the group: 1) Be kind. This does not mean you are not welcome to share your truth. This means, be kind. This is the most important rule here and anywhere. 2) Expect advice when you ask for it. If you post asking for opinions, don’t be surprised to get some opinions that you don’t like (and remember we are not doctors). Some comments may even upset you. These are opinions. Use what you can, and throw the rest away with the trash. But be kind. 3) If someone posts about an action or belief that goes against your common sense or belief system, your options are to scroll on or offer your opinion in a non-confrontational manner. Be kind. 4) Know that everything is a trigger for someone, somewhere. If you are feeling easily triggered on a particular day, it may not be the best time for you to be on Facebook. We cannot edit everyone’s responses to keep one member feeling good, nor would we want to do that. Remember to be kind. 5) This group was not formed (by Rose Armenta) to be a source of income for those who have businesses of any kind. The only members we seek are those who are looking to obtain and share friendly support. Likewise, do not offer “freebees” as a way of drumming up business at a later date. There are more appropriate places for that than an anxiety support page. Be kind, and do not take advantage of the suffering of others. On this, we will have zero tolerance. 6) It is OK to mention your faith, but keep in mind that our group is open to the entire world – with lots of faiths, practices and religions. We embrace everyone here. Be kind. In that same vein, DO NOT PUT YOUR POSTS IN ALL CAPS. THIS IS THE ONLINE EQUIVALENT OF YELLING. 7) Finally, if any member discusses bodily harm in any way, be supportive and offer the suicide prevention hotline number provided as our profile picture (or 911, or the country’s equivalent, as necessary). Note: It really is impossible to tell online when someone is seriously considering hurting themselves. Always be kind. .. Thank you so very much for your awesome contribution to our membership! We count on you!! Sincerely, your administration: Rose Armenta (founder), Jenna Alexandra, Kimberly Bloir, Julz Burcher, Jessica Colmenero, Asfand Durrani, Rose Lopez, Sina Montano and Zoe Parker

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 American Sign Language (ASL)
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to America Sign Language. Your joining this group where the Admins from this page is Deaf and Hard of Hearing also members who are here to help as well, who willing to take theirs timeout to teach you guys ASL and the culture itself. When you join a group or for example Walk into your friend home, What do you do? Respect them and theirs rules whether you agreed or not. Its not your place to say so. Just like we walk into your home, We have to respect you and your rules even if we disagree. Our focus is on the learning of ASL for the purpose of communicating with Deaf and Hard of Hearing individuals. We recognize the close relationship between ASL and Deaf Culture, and realize that it is virtually impossible to separate the two, that a person cannot study one without learning about the other. Thus we ask that all members show respect for Deaf Culture and members of the Deaf Community who are involved with this group. We have a rich diversity of members that spans different age groups, backgrounds, and levels of experience, knowledge, and skill. Some of our members are taking or have taken courses on the university level, while others are self-teaching themselves using books, on-line programs and other resources. Some of our members are themselves D/deaf or Hard of Hearing. Such diversity can sometimes make for challenging discussions and negative feelings—but we encourage members to hang in there, work through it, and most importantly to communicate with one another and respect each other. We also recognize that people may have different reasons for being interested in learning and using ASL. While we respect those various reasons, we ask that everyone carefully analyze their own reasons in order to determine whether this group best meets their needs and interests. While we welcome all who are interested, we also agree that this group may not be for everyone. Thank you Please answer those approval/deny questions... if you don't you will not be approve, again thanks...

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Bipolar Disorder Support Group - A Global Community
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to our group! We ask you to answer all group questions before accepting you into the group. We do not accept members that have not answered all questions. **When you join the group, the first thing we ask you to do is read the rules posted in our announcement section. This is VERY important as it outlines all of our rules!** Since being founded in the summer of 2013 we have subsequently grown into the largest bipolar disorder discussion group on the internet and we would love to have you join us! While our group is very large, the support for all our group members is not dwarfed by the population. You will find people from all walks of life and situations here. This group is not focused on us as admins, but on you, the members. This is a safe space for those of us with bipolar disorder to have frank discussions about our lives and what we are dealing with. Remember, you have a disorder, not a character flaw! :) When you have bipolar disorder, you often have to go about life covering up how you truly feel to please others. This is where you can really let everyone know how you are really feeling. Trust me, we get it. Thanks for joining! I hope you find what you are looking for in here. Note: We only add accounts which are over 30 days old.

Hindi mag-comply, hindi po marereview ang application* Ang "online community" na ito ay binubuo ng mga ina, ama, trained breastfeeding peer counselors, breastfeeding experts, at mga espesyalista sa pangangalaga ng kalusugan ng sanggol, bata at buntis. Naglalayon ang Breastfeeding Pinays na makapagbigay ng wastong kaalaman, suporta at lakas ng loob para sa mga inang gusto magpasuso (breastfeeding), bumalik sa pagpapasuso (relactation) at matuto ng tamang impormasyon tungkol sa pagpapasuso. Inaasam din ng grupong ito na maitaguyod ang pagpapasuso bilang pamantayan ng bawat pamilyang Pilipino - Protect, Promote and Support Breastfeeding. Maaring sagutan po ang membership questions at basahin ang rules and guidelines ng grupo para sa mga nais maging miyembro ng Breastfeeding Pinays.

                 Alcoholics Anonymous
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 {{ PLEASE READ BEFORE POSTING }} This is not an official AA group. This is a Facebook group discussing AA, Alcoholism, and Recovery. The group is open for anyone to join, and anyone can see that you are a member. If you are posting things here that could get you fired or divorced, it’s on you; you have been informed. Alcoholism is a sickness, an illness, a malady. There is no known cure, but it can be arrested – it can be stopped in its tracks. This is a place for people to talk realistically &amp; honestly about AA's solution, as well as their own experience with implementing AA in their daily life. AM I ALCOHOLIC? If, when you honestly want to, you find you cannot quit entirely, or if when drinking, you have little control over the amount you take, you are probably alcoholic. Only you can decide if you are alcoholic. LINKS: No promoting of sites. Refrain from posting links to treatment centers, self-help books, religious material, etc. PICTURES: No pictures. This is a discussion board, not a photo board; please help us keep it that way. COPYRIGHT: Please avoid posting copywriten material. This includes quotes from your favorite treatment center handbook, links to bootlegged treatment center videos, and all other things of this nature. Many people plug in brief quotes form AA literature; so far this has not been an issue, and we have not been asked to stop. Keep these kind of quotes brief, and please make sure they are being used in relation to your experience. Links to recovery talks has not yet become an issue either, as long as you’re not promoting the site hosting the talks. CONDUCT: There are more requirements than just to have a desire to stop drinking. No trolling. No harassment. No swearing at or deliberate insulting of other members or their views. No spamming, including multiple postings and dominating the page. There are over 13,000 members. If your face appears next to 50% of the new posts, or if you are posting three responses to every post, you will be asked to stop. People who violate the code of respectful conduct will be asked to stop or to leave. In certain cases of exceptional abuse, no warning will be given, and you will be permanently banned. All of these rules come down to a single word: RESPECT. Repeated flaming will you get KickBanned: http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Flaming_(Internet) Trolling will get you KickBanned: http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Internet_trolling Spammers will be immediately KickBanned: http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spamming FINALLY: If you are alcoholic, and you want to get better, go to a meeting, get a sponsor, take the twelve steps, seek a higher power, and try to make it to bed tonight without a drink. If you are not able to get to a meeting, or get a sponsor, the following guys are one of many, many people who can help you with taking the 12 steps: Joe and Charlie Big Book study: http://www.xa-speakers.org/pafiledb.php?action=category&amp;id=13

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Global Health
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 In 1804, the earth's human population reached a milestone, when the 1 billionth person was born. Today, 207 years later, 6.9 billion people reside on the planet. By the year 2050, the human population will reach 9.3 billion, and that is if the total fertility rate worldwide continues to fall (if it does not, the population in 2050 could reach 12 billion). What will the quality of life be for all these individuals. To answer that question requires an understanding of many disciplines of knowledge, including human health and disease, the environment, access to healthcare systems and medicines, access to family planning services, gender inequalities, violence and conflict worldwide, and global economic policies. This is a subject of importance to all individuals who view themselves as members of a global human community.
                </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Show Me Your Stethoscope | A Nation of Nurses
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to the official Show Me Your Stethoscope (SMYS) group! SMYS has come to be a powerful force of advocacy and support for nurses, rising above the role of traditional trade associations and politics as usual. Our motto, nurses take care of patients, we take care of nurses. Please answer the 3 questions to join. Once you're in the group, complete rules for posting can be found in the announcements. We're glad you're here! #NursesUnite #NationOfNurses #Nursing #HealthCare Condensed Rules/Guidelines for posting: 1. We're all in this together to create a welcoming environment. Let's treat everyone with respect. Disagreeing is fine and natural, but you can disagree respectfully. Name calling and insults are not necessary. Doxxing, in any form or fashion, is strictly forbidden. 2. While this group is primarily healthcare professionals, we still don't allow medical advice or diagnosing. The best thing to do is to see your doctor or go to your local urgent care. That being said, once you have a diagnosis and treatment plan. please post it so we can all learn from it! 3. While this is a closed group, we still need to be mindful of HIPAA. While your post may not violate HIPAA, there is a potential for it to violate any social media policy set forth by your facility. We just don't want you to get into any trouble if someone you work with is in this group. 4. We want to discuss what you want to discuss. However, there are a few hot button topics that are not allowed: politics (unless relates to healthcare), abortion, vaccines (unless posting EBP), anything that bashes other nurses/healthcare workers/facilities. This also extends to fake news and conspiracy theories. 5.Sales, self promotion, and personal blogs are allowed with permission. Please contact Alicia Staffier by email: Alley.staffier@gmail.com to discuss arrangements. Job postings are not allowed at this time. 6. Admins will delete a post that has been posted numerous times before. It’s nothing personal, just trying to keep fresh information available to you all. 7. Thanks to a few bad apples when this group first started, we do not allow donation sites I.e. GoFundMe, YouCaring, etc. This also goes for contest posts. 8. Please use reliable sites for posting and sharing. If your link is suspect, it will not be approved. 9. Graphic images and the like are ok as long as they stay within a PG13 guideline. Let’s put it this way- if it can be shown on “The Walking Dead” it can stay. If it hits “Game of Thrones” it can’t be posted. 10. We can not allow screenshots of test or book questions due to copyright laws. If you would like to type out the question and ask for the rationale, we will be happy to allow that post through (please don't give the name of the book/program). Also, check out our student page!
                </div>

                 The Fast Metabolism Diet Group
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 WELCOME to the largest and most active Facebook Support Group for The Fast Metabolism Diet. This group is not affiliated with Haylie Pomroy or the Haylie Pomroy Group in any way. We follow and promote the plan as Haylie has written - making any changes and updates that her team gives us along the way. We have guidelines and a no tolerance policy in this group re: promotion, self-promotion, advertising, recruiting, market research/surveying and soliciting of any kind. The ONLY exception to this is by getting admin approval PRIOR to posting. We're glad you're here!! You'll find tons of support in this group to help you navigate through the FMD. We provide a forum to post questions, share weight loss milestones, photos, recipes and anything helpful to members. Interested in one of Haylie's other plans? You're in luck! We have sister groups to support those plans too! This is a CLOSED GROUP; which means you'll have to request to join, but we will approve your request within a day. It also means that only members of this group can see the posts and comments that you make. What is FMD? FMD is an eating plan that consists of three phases a week. Each Phase focuses on different whole, healthy foods to calm your adrenal glands, reduce stress on your liver, and feed your thyroid so it can produce the hormones T3 and T4, the superstars of a fast metabolism. You’ll reduce stress too—and as a result, put the damper on the belly-fat hormone, cortisol. By keeping your metabolism guessing by changing phases each week, you’ll get it working faster. This isn’t just a theory; it’s the results-based product of Haylie Pomroy’s successful program. For more information about the FMD, please refer to Haylie's website at http://www.hayliepomroy.com.

We want to let everyone know that are not affiliated with the Chopra Center/ Deepak/ Oprah etc in anyway. This page was started at the beginning of the 21 day series with the Chopra Center around the year of 2011. We have carefully and lovingly continued to grow over the years. We want to make sure those interested in joining that this page know that this page is not affiliated with nor a part of the Chopra Center/ Deepak Chopra Organization nor Oprah Winfrey Organizations. Our members are from all over the world and are an active group. We all share inspiring photos, quotes, meditations and support each other in group meditations and challenges. We respectfully ask all our members to not advertise their products or services directly on our page. However, starting 2019, we are bringing forward some of our members that are experienced meditation teachers to offer mini series between the Chopra Center 21 Day meditation series offered 5 times a year. We are so happy that the Chopra Center offers these to the world for free so that we meditators can enjoy in community. Please join our community but requesting and answering the new membership questions posted on the join link. If you have any direct questions you can message one our communications admin April Perkinson or Monica Soto. April Perkinson is our new members admin. WELCOME and NAMASTE April Perkinson Monica Soto

PLEASE READ AND FOLLOW THESE GUIDELINES: http://bit.ly/2ygavJK The only exception to these guidelines are that you CAN post housing in this group and all other travel nurse conversations/photos will be deleted and should be discussed in the Travel Nurse Network ( https://www.facebook.com/groups/TheGypsyNurseNetwork/). DISCLAIMER: Group Members – please note: the housing opportunities in this group are not owned or managed by The Gypsy Nurse. The Gypsy Nurse is not responsible for any housing-related agreements or issues between those seeking housing and those offering housing. Any housing arrangements, communication or action between parties in this group are entered into at the risk of those parties and The Gypsy Nurse is not responsible for any aspect of those arrangements, communication or action. ATTENTION: We do screen ALL profiles so there is still a chance that spammers will get in even though it is a closed group. We always recommend that you NOT share personal contact info, addresses, etc on the public post and share it only via PM. If you have job needs please post them to the Jobs group here:https://www.facebook.com/groups/GypsyNurseJobs/ We also invite your to join in on our Main Network group for additional support and conversation:https://www.facebook.com/groups/TheGypsyNurseNetwork/ We also have a Housing Tool http://www.thegypsynurse.com/housing-list/

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Weight Loss Support Group - Friendly and Free Drama!
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Real weight-loss requires a good healthy diet and exercise. Our members all have great information on how they have achieved their goals. If you are looking to lose weight and live a healthy lifestyle then this will be the perfect group. Absolutely NO SELLING of weight loss drinks, pills, magic potions, miracle drugs. Any indication of this type of activity will get you banned and blocked immediately. No pming members, asking to be pmed, group chats, posting links to you, groups, social media accounts, etc. This is a REAL weight loss group and we intend to keep it that way. 18+ no exceptions. Thanks! A copy of the rules: 1. WHAT WE'RE ABOUT. This is a page for Weight Loss. It's not strictly one program of any kind, though many of us are counting calories or carbs, and can provide help. We are supporters of healthy ways to lose weight. Not every post is weight loss related which is why we are Weight Loss &amp; More. Staying on topic is our main goal. 2. WE CURSE. GET USED TO IT. If you aren't okay with that, you may not like it here. Some of us WILL offend you ~ most likely an Admin/Mod. Prepare yourself. We have good hearts &amp; mean well, but tend to lack filters. 3. NO JUDGING. We do not judge the food choices of others, since we are all on different plans. We are all here to support each other. If you see something you disagree with, just keep scrolling. Remember this doesn't mean members can't express concern if you post something that looks very unhealthy/dangerous to your health. 4. NO SELLING OF ANY KIND. DON'T ASK. No It Works ( it doesn't ), No Herbalife ( GetaLife), No Plexus ( nothing rhymes with Plexus ). Just NO. If you try to sell, you will be banned from the group. No questions asked. 5. NO RANDOM FRIEND REQUESTS OR MESSAGING. No one likes getting friend requests or PM's from random people. It either makes you a creeper or a seller - neither of which we do allow. We also do not allow group chats. You will be banned. 6. NO "FAD" DIETS, DETOXES, ACV ( APPLE CIDER VINEGAR), PILLS OR POTIONS. We don't support " fad diets" here. You can be on one, but don't expect positive feedback on it. We are more about a long-term lifestyle change rather than a short term "quick fix" or diet. 7. NO POSTING LINKS TO "YOU". No links to outside sources such as blogs, groups, pages, channels, profiles, etc. Where you are the owner. This group is for the support of our members, and not for your profit. Your link will be trolled. 8. FEEL FREE TO BE "OFF TOPIC". Some groups require that you stay "on topic". We do not. Not everything in your journey must be serious &amp; that not everything in your life must be weight loss related. "Off topic" posts are ok. 9. HAVE FUN. When in doubt, don't be a douche. That's Adrian's job. That's it. Have fun! 10. No blocking Admins/Mods If you block one of us you will be automatically banned

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Aidan Jack Seeger
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 235 children will be born with Adrenoleukodystrophy (ALD) every year in this country alone. With Newborn Screening these children can be monitored and saved from the affects of this devastating disease. Our son, Aidan jack, was diagnosed with ALD on June 2, 2011; he was just 6 years old. ALD is a horrific metabolic disease, which affects the myelin sheath in the brain and affects all neurological functioning, eventually leading to death. Aidan was in 1st grade, above grade level and running and playing as any child his age. He started having vision problems around April and we just assumed he needed glasses. After many doctors and finally an MRI and a VLCFA blood test, Aidan was diagnosed with ALD. The only option to possibly stop the progression of the disease is a bone marrow transplant. Aidan received his unrelated cord blood transplant at Duke University in North Carolina on July 21, 2011, also his 7th birthday. The months that followed were grueling, the bone marrow transplant was a success, but unfortunately, since Aidan was already symptomatic and with the effects of chemotherapy and the disease progressing, all took its toll. Aidan lost his vision, hearing, ability to eat and walk and communicate. After 10 months in the hospital, our baby lost his life on April 29, 2012. If New York and the rest of the nation had ALD added to Newborn Screening, Aidan and so many others could have been saved. On March 29, 2013 New York became the 1st state to add ALD to the newborns screening panel. Starting January 1, 2014 every baby born in New York State will be tested for ALD giving them the best possible chance for a normal healthy life. Aidan Jack Seeger Foundation was started in 2012 to help advocate for EVERY state to screen newborns for ALD To help families affected by ALD To raise awareness and support research for a cure Together we can fight for the nation to screen for ALD and save these boys from this horrific disease. www.aidanhasaposse.org Thank you for your support!!! 
                </div>

                 Keto Yourself Skinny
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Keto Yourself Skinny (KYS) is a group for those interested on the Ketogenic Diet. We call it a diet but it is a way of life. It's not just about weight loss, it's about better living, more energy, clarity and a healthier attitude. Please use the search function before posting a question. We post recipes every day to help provide inspiration and shortcut your meal planning. We actively encourage you to share recipes (not links to menu plans - these are mostly spam) that work for you or you particularly enjoy to help others in the group. This is a zero spam or selling zone. Do not post links to your own blogs or other Facebook groups. 1. Ask lots of questions. Everyone wants to help you grow. 2. Please do not post ANY non-recipe links. There is so much misinformation out there we just delete them. You risk being banned from the group. 3. Please do not post links to any keto menus. Those are often spam sites. 4. Please do not try to sell anything in the group. This means your own or any other link. 5. Please do not try to convince us to use keto drink products. 6. Please be kind to our fellow members. 7. If we no longer serve your purposes and you choose to leave, we wish you well. 8. Cheat posts of any kind will be deleted. We expect you to take full responsibility for what goes into your mouth. Cheat posts that encourage others will cause you to be immediately removed. Supporting cheat posts is not in the best interests of the members and may result in you being removed from the group. 9. If you are stuck or have a problem, please ask. 10. Please DO post recipe links. Make sure they are 100% keto friendly before posted. Do not suggest substitutions. Non-keto recipes will be removed from our group. 11. If anyone private messages you offering to sell you something, block them and let us know. Please do no actively solicit for friend requests within the group. 12. Andrew is the main admin of the group. 13. Hosting Watch Parties or Sharing videos of MLM or other reps who solicit likes and shares is strictly forbidden without prior approval from Admin. You risk being removed from the group. 15. If an admin or moderator says a product is not Keto, do not respond "But it works for me." 16. From time to time, KYS or one of the team may post links to products they think are of value. You may assume that some of these links are affiliate links. KYS and team only recommend products they or the members of the group believe in.. Enjoy! Andrew.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Baby and Childhood Eczema Support Group
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 A support group for parents and caregivers of babies, toddlers and young children with eczema. It can be a frustrating minefield trying to find information and this group is a safe place to share tips and ideas regarding diet, skin and laundry products, associated allergies, mainstream or natural treatments, etc. Not everything will work for everyone but let's share, empathise and make suggestions so it's not such a lonely battle. Please note that any information shared is based on 'research' or personal experience and it would be advisable to consult your child's medical practitioner too for diagnosis and treatment. We are not qualified to give or moderate medical advice and are not responsible for the accuracy of any advice given within the group. Please desist from advertising or self promotion as we would like to remain objective and impartial. It is fine to make recommendations based on your own findings or experiences. Please DO NOT send private messages to group members promoting products. Anyone advertising or promoting themselves or someone they know will be removed from the group without warning. Please help by notifying an admin about any private messages you receive. It is okay to recommend mainstream products that you use on your child where there is no personal or financial gain to you or someone you know. In addition, please DO NOT recommend or promote any individual or specific medical practitioners or online doctors. Apart from the risks of certain treatments being high or largely untested, we are against supporting the financial gain of any particular individual as objectivity may be compromised. We want to keep this group as safe as possible. Any concerns please let us know. Child protection is a priority here so please do not post any intimate, naked or full body shots of your child's eczema. Please crop respectfully to preserve the dignity and safety of your child. Please be polite even if you disagree with the views or choices of other members. Any rudeness or personal attacks will result in removal from the group. Please do not discourage other parents from using topical steroids. It is permitted to give advice about proper use of steroids to avoid skin complications but not to discourage all steroid use. In addition, please do not discourage other parents on this platform from taking up infant immunisations. Any anti-vaccination posts will be deleted along with the originator. Please do not recommend the use of essential oils. They have caused a disproportionate number of babies in this group to flare. Admins will delete anything at their discretion if they deem it inappropriate or unsafe. We hope you find this group helpful and that others will benefit from your participation, support and personal experience too.

Games are allowed, but can be deleted at Admin's discretion. 10. Members may not offer OR receive donations of any kind, asked for or otherwise. Fundraisers are not allowed.                  RxPrep CPJE Study Group
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Hi everyone. We wanted to create a place where students studying for the law portion of the CPJE can connect with other students in their area and form study groups, share study tips and compare notes. To avoid loss of your license, do NOT post actual board exam questions or copyrighted material, including entire book pages (e.g., from any of the RxPrep Course Books). Asking questions from/about material in copyrighted books is acceptable. We do not want our students to be engaged in any unlawful, unethical practice. If actual board questions are discussed in this group, the poster and anyone discussing them has violated ethical practice, and has jeopardized the right to practice as a pharmacist. Thank you for helping us maintain a high standard of legal and ethical practice. The RxPrep CPJE Course can be purchased here: https://www.rxprep.com/store/products/125/rxprep-2019-california-law-summary-for-cpje-online-course Welcome to the RxPrep CPJE Study Group! Please do not comment “F” on a thread. It is overloading other students with notifications. There is a small arrow located in the upper-right corner of the post. Click on the arrow and select “Turn on notifications for this post” from the drop-down menu.

You do not have to be certified to be listed on the BirthTUBE Directory. https://birthtubelive.com + I posted to the BirthTUBE Group wall, where is my post? Great question, we try to keep BirthTUBE organized by reserving the BirthTUBE feed for Live Mama’s, Admin announcements and recorded birth videos. The @Birthtube Sister group is open discussion and a great place to ask questions! Birth story/photos? + How do I know when a birth is live? Make sure you have “ALL NOTIFICATIONS” turned on or you can sign up to receive a text message. + How do I receive a text message when a birth is live? Text Follow @birthtube to the number 40404 (you do not have to have a twitter to receive a text update. However, it doesn’t work for everyone.) + Hey, I signed up for text message updates but I am not receiving them. What should I do? The texting service is free so it is unpredictable .                <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 subtle asian mental health
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Thank you for becoming a member of our community! We hope that you find this to be an open, safe, inclusive, and non-judgmental space to share your thoughts and feelings about anything, especially mental health. Please acknowledge that while we would like to be inclusive, this space is primarily a place for Asians and those of Asian descent. Our hope for this group is to reach as many Asians struggling with mental health, cultural issues, inter-generational trauma, and associated problems as possible. We want Asians to realize they are not alone in their struggles and experiences and that there are others who are here to provide support. Mental health is a growing issue among global Asian diaspora communities, but as Asians we tend to be brought up to not talk about it or even acknowledge our psychological problems. We want to be a part of the generation that changes that, and we hope you'll come along with us for this journey. We've prepared some resources for you, which you can find in either the announcements or files tab on the left hand sidebar. Some of them include: – Subtle Asian Confessions – Listening Sessions – Resources on Mental Health **Comments will be heavily moderated. Problematic comments may warrant a PM from mods/admins and may or may not be deleted. We encourage "good" discourse, which means people can disagree but everyone should treat each other with respect. We do not tolerate racism, sexism, bigotry, homophobia, transphobia, etc, but we should educate others with empathy and compassion. For more information about what else we do, check out our website: https://www.asianmhc.org/
                </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Massage Therapists
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This is an OPEN group. Read this entire description, then read the comments below the post pinned to the top of this page. We are predominantly Massage Therapists that care about their profession and wish to discuss what we do. We respect one another, but do not expect everyone to agree. We welcome open debate and the presentation of evidence for/against any concept/practice. Wear your thinking cap and be willing to accept that you may be wrong about something. We are all adults here, and adult behavior is expected. Childish behavior (whining, tantrums, name-calling, etc.) will not be condoned. This is a professional discussion page, not a playground. Professionals representing other health/fitness professions are also welcome. This includes PTs, DCs, MDs, DOs, ATCs, personal trainers, etcetera. We all share a common goal: To improve the health of our clients/patients and encourage healthy habits. Trolls, spam, advertising for products/classes, and such are prohibited. This page is for discussion, not for sales. If a link to information about a class/product is directly relevant to a discussion, that's fine. Repeat offenders will be permanently banned. This group is not about treating every opinion and idea as equally valid. We're not here for a group hug. For a profession to advance, it must discard outdated/disproven/untenable ideas. This short video on "Open-Mindedness" may be helpful for orientation purposes: http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=T69TOuqaqXI This video on "Critical Thinking" may also be helpful: http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6OLPL5p0fMg This OPEN forum is a place for professional growth via professional DISCUSSIONS and DEBATES related to Massage Therapy. The posts should share information/ideas, ask questions without fear of reproach and/or provide more than very basic advice. Please review the pinned post (https://www.facebook.com/groups/611431842200765/permalink/611508235526459/) for what the forum is about, and some aspects of the culture encouraged here. The admins (https://www.facebook.com/groups/611431842200765/admins) are here to help with questions about etiquette, and ensure that the forum rules are met. If you wish to post a question anonymously, an admin will be happy to do it for you. Please make sure that the question has all the information the responders will need, to give you the best advice. You MAY not get an opportunity to respond on the conversation, without revealing your identity. The admins do not monitor every response in a post. Please report posts that break rules of etiquette, especially inappropriate posts, and personal attacks. It speeds up resolving problems early before they escalate. Use the "report to admin" option to remain anonymous, and/or PM two or more admins, or tag two or more us in a response. Everyone's ideas and enthusiasm are welcome. However we will remove posts that do not fit this group's intended culture. If your post is removed, check which rule has been violated.

                 Meditation Matters
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Thank you all for being part of our Meditation Matters family! Admins - Jennifer Cortis &amp; Edward Niam This group welcomes anyone interested in the art of meditation and the benefits of regular practice and various methods to improve your mental, physical and spiritual health. Regardless of the type of training you are involved with or if you do nothing at all, you need to meditate daily to bring balance back in your life and hear the music inside of you. Meditation is the Yin energy contrasting the Yang of physical exercise. The proper mix of Yin and Yang energy is necessary for optimal mental, physical and spiritual health. Regular meditation will relieve tension and stress, release anxiety, create a mind-body connection, enhance focus and awareness, release energy blocks, gain a sense of calmness and well-being, lessen mood swings, balance metabolism and blood pressure, increase Chi (vital energy) and develop a deeper understanding of yourself and the world around you. What is it that we give our children every day when they are young - something to help them calm down, reflect on their activities of the day and connect with their inner self? For you modern day parents, I'm not talking about Ritalin. The answer is Quiet Time. For a child, Quiet Time is a natural form of meditation. How many of us get Quiet Time every day? The best Quiet Time for an adult is to practice some form of meditation regularly. Consistency is important because meditation is like an exercise. The more you practice, the better you get. Please note that all members are invited to submit posts. They are important and we look forward to reading them, however, please limit your submissions to 2 per day. And regarding Comments on Posts, please keep them respectful, positive and helpful. About our Admins: Reverend Edward Niam, DD is a Grand Master of Shaolin Kung Fu, Tai Chi Chuan, Pa Kua Chang, Acpuncture, Tui Na and Meditation &amp; has been helping people utilize the secrets of alternative health &amp; wellness therapies for 45 years. Pastor of Spiritual Inspiration Ministries &amp; a Motivational Speaker. Jennifer Cortis is the founder of Lotus Room Yoga Centre in Malta. Jennifer is a gifted teacher, practitioner, innovator and leader. Jennifer is well known for her knowledge, skill and understanding of all forms of Meditation. She also conducts workshops and retreats globally. GUIDELINES FOR POST SUBMISSION: We welcome all posts related to meditation, health, wellness &amp; all complimentary modalities as well as events, services, products and training programs. Posts asking for money donations will be rejected as will anything promoting a particular religion or political viewpoint, gambling/lottery, chain style posts, profanity &amp; anything deemed inappropriate. Also, posts must be in English or accompanied by a translation. Advertising in the “Comment” section of someone else’s post is not permitted. All inappropriate submissions will be deleted and the user blocked.

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Dyslexia Group. Increase awareness and understanding.
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Increase awareness and understanding of the effects of dyslexia ... Bring together those involved with dyslexic adults and children to discuss ways… and the aim to bring about a dyslexia friendly society. Please have a look at these petitions, they mean a lot to me. https://you.38degrees.org.uk/p/katherinegleeson https://petition.parliament.uk/petitions/168137 I started the group to aim to encourage organizations and individuals to work together represent the needs of dyslexic people, that we can work together to raise awareness of dyslexia… support all to reach their full potential as audience or members, to take positive action to achieve this. To work with others in the aim to bring about improvements and build a wider group of people the opportunity to do ... meaning to a much wider audience than the individual alone. I'm hopeful that we can make this happen together. Founder and Campaigner, Katherine Gleeson, Dyslexic, Dyspraxia , Dyscalculia and Asperger's ...... welcome to the group x Petition's the UK Government More training for teachers and more specialists for hidden conditions. Multiply Your Impact Turn your signature into dozens sharing your petition and recruiting people you know to sign. Why not set up a petition and we will post here. Thousands of children and young adults across the UK are being neglected or undetected by the Education System due to lack of knowledge and proper means of support for conditions such as Dyspraxia, Dyslexia, Dysgraphia, Dyscalculia, Apraxia, ADHD, Autism, Epilepsy, Diabetes etc. Waiting lists to see the specialists for diagnosis are extremely long. Many parents and young adults are confused and "fobbed off" by schools and Further Education establishments due to the staff's lack of knowledge about these conditions and many feel like their concerns are not being heard or acted upon. The current system makes it difficult to know where to turn as many are told to see their GP, who then refers them back to the school. I believe that by providing further training, both to existing staff within the Education system and introducing it into Teacher Training programmes then fewer children and young adults will go un-noticed. With greater levels of Occupational Therapists and Paediatricians, those affected will be seen quicker and the support required can be provided sooner, making the problems with levels of stress (for both parents and those with the condition) and low self esteem less. Admin :;from 2010 Ranjit Kumar Holly Muzzy. Robert Keane, Michael Matteucig Distinquel Etude Soci, Individualment Aprendizagem. 2011 Corinna Shepherd R.I.P, Lakshmi Shankar,Jo Taylor. 2012 Janet Bennison 2013 kapie 2013 Richard Hall, 22/05/2013 Sue Whiting. 2014 Sarah Chapman, Kimberley Crites 2015 Jennifer flack,Charlotte Ward. 2015 Walter Dunson ,Emma Fitzgerald.                <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Mindful Living
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 We live in such a fast-paced world with SO much to pay attention to. This often leaves us feeling overwhelmed, stressed, dissatisfied, and disconnected. So how can mindfulness help? Mindfulness is the intentional focus of awareness (attention) on the present moment, without our automatic filters and lenses of judgment. It involves being in connection with the direct experience of the here and now. As you work on bringing more mindfulness into your life, you'll train your mind to break free from the routine of daily life by intentionally priming it for good, creating a more resilient brain so that you can manage life's inevitable difficulties with greater ease and clarity, while feeling more connected to the world around you. This is a secular group is for anyone who is interested in learning about integrating more mindfulness into daily life to cultivate a greater sense of peace, compassion, and happiness moment-to-moment. GUIDELINES AND REQUIREMENTS We have a few guidelines and requirements for participating in the group and posting on the wall: 1) We welcome your posts and discussions around mindfulness and mindful living but please know that overtly promotional posts will be removed, and repeated instances of this will result in our need to excuse you from the group. 2) Promotion of other groups (Facebook and otherwise), blogs, courses, or programs is NOT permitted. If you have information that you feel will genuinely benefit this group, please send the details to one of the group administrators for consideration. * Only group admins are permitted to post about outside groups, courses or programs. * 3) If you post an affiliate link, you MUST state in your post that it's an affiliate link - we will check for redirects and cloaking. These posts must also be relevant and genuinely useful for the group. Again, if posting affiliate links becomes a habit, we'll need to excuse you from the group. 4) Unless someone has explicitly asked for a PM in the group, please refrain from sending unsolicited messages to other group members. If you engage in this practice, we'll need to excuse you from the group. 5) Please do not ever solicit donations or funding (however well-intended) due to the high risk of scamming. We want everyone's interaction here to provide a living wisdom for us all to benefit from! Thank you for adhering to our guidelines for this community!
