               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 LOW CARB EATING
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to Low Carb Eating! LCE members collectively define Low Carb Eating as 20 to 50 carbs a day total for fat loss and maintenance. There is no one set eating plan here, however, each member follows their choice of any Low Carb Plan they've chosen for themselves through personal research. What is acceptable on their plan may not be on yours so please be aware of this and be respectful of other's choices. However, encouraging others to eat sugar, starches, pastas, and fruits will not be tolerated since a serving of these foods can easily exceed most members daily carb quota, spike blood sugar, cause stalls, and promote weight gain. Carb Cycling posts are not allowed. If you cheat, reaching out for support is fine but DO NOT mention the foods you ate. These can discourage or trigger others. Videos are not allowed. This is a political and religion free zone and any posts or comments will be removed if we see them!. This group is a positive, safe, non-judgmental place to share meal plans, progress, encouragement, mutual support, and empowerment. Our Admins are Sheila Ecker, Kat Morris, Brandy Redeker, Kerin Kay, Lori Ellin and Shirley Girard. We are always happy to help! (Take note that no member is to block an administrator. If so, they will be removed. Our group is privately owned and memberships are granted &amp; revoked under that discretion. We are not doctors. Members who are in the medical profession are asked that they refrain from giving medical advice to anyone in the group. Please encourage others to do their own research instead. PLEASE NOTE: Our group focus is Low Carb Eating and Food. For exercise and fitness support please visit LCFG Fitness Group at https://www.facebook.com/groups/1620261574883533/ Report any inappropriate content. The Admins do their best to catch everything as soon as possible but keep in mind we get about 100 requests to join a day and it is not possible to investigate each individually and know if they will cause trouble or not. This is not a place to advertise your products, services, pages, or other groups so please do not post advertisements, product endorsements, fitness challenges, or any other posts for likes, members, or monetary gain. Do not contact members through private message to solicit. That is a gross misuse of trust and if it is reported the offender will get banned. MINIMUM AGE REQUIREMENT is 18 because Eating Disorders that fuel a dieting mentality is so rampant with teens today. Nothing is thin enough, the thigh gap can't be big enough, the stomach can't be flat enough, etc. As a group we do not want to be negatively contributing to the mental health and/or body image issues of a minor so we ask that group members are 18 and over. If you are a parent working with your child(ren) on this WOE, you are welcome to share those experiences here. However, minors are not allowed to be actual members of the group. ~ Low Carb Eating -

Welcome to our group. We have a wide spectrum of diversity here. In order to keep things peaceful, we have the following guidelines. All members are expected to abide by these rules. If you cannot, please find a group better suited to your needs. • No profanity • No "looking for love" posts. • No religious posts (for or against any religion) • No spam, ads, "gofundme" or MLM posts. • No nudity or porn. • No trolling or flaming. • No personal info: VP/phone numbers, email addresses, etc. Share this kind of thing in private.                  This group is for Calm Subscribers who want to explore and discuss the themes presented in the Daily Calm (a 10-minute mindfulness meditation written by Tamara Levitt, and served fresh daily in the Calm App). We aim to be one of the kindest and most inspiring places on the internet by deepening in awareness and equanimity. We cultivate a sense of connection based on mindfulness, nurturing a calm place within, and celebrating the beauty that surrounds us. You can learn more about Calm here: bit.ly/DAILYCALM The intention of this group is to cultivate a sense of connection based on our shared mindfulness practice. There’s an abundance of experience, knowledge, and heart in our global community of meditators. Let’s learn from each other and grow together. You’re invited to share your mindfulness insights, talk about what comes up for you in your meditation, how you integrate mindfulness into your daily life, offer encouragement, and ask questions. We ask that all sharing be done through the lens of mindfulness. We know this is a practice, you don’t have to be perfect, just open to exploring the process with us.                 <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Support Group for parents with kids with ADHD, ADD, Autism and other issues
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to the group new members!! Please take a minute to read the description below about this group. I hope you find it helpful to be here. This group is a place to give support, and to recommend strategies to other members, post ONLY things related to ADHD, ADD, Autism and behavior issues. This group is aware of HIPAA, so even though you are not required to state your child’s diagnosis in your post, we need to remind you that it is helpful to other members in order to better help you answer your questions. It is also a place to vent, BUT related to the topic. If the post does not relate to the group I will automatically delete the post. If you want to post an article, please do so with a comment, otherwise it will be deleted. It will also be nice if you say something as to why do you think the article is interesting to you or how it will help others. This way, we know you are not a spammer...if you are in this group is because you need advice among other things. Please NO sales, NO sales ads, NO advertising, NO contests and No funding an PM’ing other members. I am sure you can post that somewhere else. On the other hand, if you want to post an event that you think it could help other members in this group (related to the group, and no sales), and/or if you would like to post a research study link, please ask for permission first. If you post without permission, it will be deleted. If you don't believe ADD, ADHD, Autism or behavior issues are real, then, this group is not for you. Be positive towards other people and treat people the way you want to be treated. in order to have harmony and no drama in this group, it is important to know how to scroll down a post and ignore it when you don’t agree with it, don’t engage in a fight, BUT do let me know what is going on so I can take care of it. We all have the right to speak our minds, but please be respectful when doing so. We are all coming from different cultures, different beliefs and different countries, therefore, what you believe is ok to say, it may not be for others. The tone or the way we use towards other members has a big impact. This means that if you are blunt and honest, please have some tact in the way you express your thoughts, and absolutely NO INSULTING to others or say bad language. All those can be reworded or re-emplaced with other words. Please beware of people that requests to add you. We have people from everywhere in the world in this group. We don't know who they are, and how they are like. I don't want anyone to be taken advantage of, or being in danger after accepting their request. We live in a dangerous world, please be careful. PLEASE let me know of any inappropriate posts or Spams. If I pm you, it is because I have questions about a post, please don't take it personally. We are here to help each other. Do you still have questions or concerns? Please PM me! And again, please, respect the group and the people in it.

                 HEALTH AND GOLDEN YEARS ARE WEALTH AND BLESSINGS 🙌💒👆
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 The beginning of good health as a blessing is knowledge and practice of healthful living. Health springs from our environment, substances we ingest, the food we eat, things we fill our minds and spirit and how we relate with others. These days it also necessitates being aware of the social dimensions of health and liberating ourselves from the excesses and abuses wrought by modern medical practice and pharmaceutical industry and their conditioning of our minds. And there is wisdom in going back to healing practices validated by time and those laws of nature ordained by God Himself. Reaching our senior years speaks so much of how good the state of our health and wellness is. But most of all, our golden years mean what a gracious God we have in Heaven for such gift of number of years He allows us to live in Him and for Him. With this group, let us exchange and freely draw from the marketplace of health and wellbeing ideas and inspirations, and be warned as well.

                  We are a group of people who value peace, tranquillity, a contented and untroubled mind, and offer this space as a refuge from this sometimes uncertain and troubled world. Please keep all comments relevant, civil, supportive, tolerant, kindly and non sectarian - we are all friends here! Out of consideration for everyone... no more than one post per day. No self promotion, spam or irrelevant links. Any questions feel free to contact the admins. Stanislaw Sieradzki &amp; Rex Boaden

                 Daughters Of Abusive Mothers
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 **Please answer ALL questions or you will not be accepted.** This group is specifically for daughters of mothers who are/were abusive (physical, mental, emotional, spiritual and/or financial abuse) or caused trauma to their children. We accept members who have or have had an abusive mother figure in their life. Whether it's an abusive mother, stepmother, foster mother, aunt, mother-in-law or a sister, if it's a maternal figure who was/is abusive, you are welcome here to vent without judgment. We are an inclusive group and if you cannot accept others as equal and regard their experiences within their own communities, do not add yourself. You don’t need to be a ciswoman to join our group! If your experience with an abusive mother figure also includes you being (past or present) a daughter figure, you are welcome! This is a support group for healing and we do not condone hateful speech against personality disorders themselves. Admin and mod team are primarily minorities such as POC, physically disabled, have mental illness including personality disorders, and LGBTQ or autistic mods. We accept all diversity in this group are always looking for new minorities for our mod team.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Tongue Ties, Autism, MTHFR, Vaccines, Leaky Gut - What's the Connection?
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 *Take a moment to answer our 3 brief questions upon requesting to join the group. Requests with unanswered questions will be declined. No exceptions. We get over 100 requests a day and it takes a really long time to go through them all. Any member requests with unanswered screening questions that remain after 24 hours will be removed. If this happens and you would still like to join the group, feel free to resubmit your request and answer the screening questions at that time. Please note that we do NOT add members without their permission.* This group is designed to help clarify the connection between tongue ties, MTHFR genetic mutations, autism, vaccine injuries, autoimmune and intestinal permeability (or leaky gut). There's so much information out there that can be very overwhelming. This is a safe place to share knowledge and research as well as ask questions. Please keep discussions civil. This group is not about being "pro" or "anti" anything - other than pro-information and pro-research. You may receive a private message request from an admin before being added to the group, so be sure to check your message request folder. Please do not add anyone without their knowledge or consent. It is against group rules to send a private message to another member without their permission to advertise products that you sell. Doing this can result in immediate removal and banning from the group. If someone wishes to join the group, they need to answer the brief entry questions to be approved or they will be declined. Disclaimer: Please seek a medical provider for diagnoses. We are not doctors and are not responsible for any advice acted upon in this group. We are mamas who are passionate about healthy living and learning about the role that our genetics play in our health.

                 Dyslexia
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 I started this group because I had reason to believe my son was dyslexic. I wish I had realized earlier that he had this disorder, everyone should pay close attention to symptoms of this. I hope to meet other parents whose children who have been diagnosed as Dyslexic so we can share ideas, what works etc. As the group has evolved I have two admins that assist me in the running and we have incorporated a set of requirements for this group – please review them before asking to join 1. This group is a supportive group. 2. Share or question from your heart. 3. Share or question from your experiences. 4. Some of you may represent companies or products please do not SPAM. 5. Spamming may incur a review of membership. 6. No flaming or spamming will be tolerated. 7. The owner and admins reserve the right to ban people. 8. Any ? ask Cherie (owner), Saskia or Vicki (admins) 9. Belittling a person because of questions will Not be tolerated. 10.Please do not Block anyone as we are ALL here to learn and get answers. Doing so causes those that are to be confused by comments on a post.

                 ➡️ PLEASE READ BEFORE POSTING: A Message from Hal Elrod, author and founder of The Miracle Morning... Welcome! The Miracle Morning COMMUNITY is made up of over 250,000+ like-minded individuals from over 100 countries, who wake up everyday and dedicate time to practicing the Miracle Morning in an effort to fulfill their own individual potential while supporting others in doing the same. Together, we are on a mission to elevate the consciousness of humanity, one morning (and one person) at a time. How? As we each elevate our own consciousness (i.e. learn, grow, and improve ourselves), we automatically elevate the consciousness of every other humanity. As we become better, humanity becomes better. Welcome to The Miracle Morning Community; I am truly grateful to be on this journey with you! With love &amp; gratitude, - Hal P.S. (Silence, Affirmations, Visualization, Exercise, Reading, Scribing). 🛑 DON'T: Promote your products, programs, "FREE" offers/invitations, blog, podcast, YouTube Channel or anything else that is self-promotional. Don't share you LIVE videos - these will no longer be approved). ✅ DO: Find an accountability partner (this does not mean start other accountability groups), and share how we can best support you with your Miracle Morning journey. 🛑 DON'T post things unrelated to The Miracle Morning (i.e. politics, business, COVID-19, quarantine, self-Isolation or anything related to the current pandemic).                  Travel Nurse Housing - Furnished Finder 💛💛
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to the Furnished Finder Facebook Group for Travel Nurse Housing! This Facebook group is heavily monitored &amp; moderated Furnished Finder, but acts independently from the Furnished Finder site and app. All group members are expected to read and follow the group rules which are posted. Travelers use our website (www.furnishedfinder.com) to find affordable furnished housing for their work assignments across the US. Hosts list their monthly furnished properties on our website (only $99 for a 12 month listing) to connect with travel nurse tenants coming to their area for work. There are no booking fees (for either party) on our website or app. Every host on the website is background checked for traveler safety (happens automatically when a property is listed). If you have a paid FF listing, please include a link within your posts so travelers know you’re verified. Hosts who post on this Facebook group without a FF link are NOT verified or confirmed by Furnished Finder. Please use caution while interacting on this, or any, Facebook group and report any suspicious posts or fake accounts to the admin. We take all reports of fraud very seriously. Property owners do not have to be a paid host on the Furnished Finder website to post on our FB group. Every ‘Housing-Offered’ post must include these 4 things to prevent it from being removed: 1) Images 2) Price 3) Location 4) Description Furnished Finder customers are encouraged to direct all Customer Service related questions to customerservice@furnishedfinder.com. Posts may be removed for not following group rules (posted separately). Members who receive multiple reports for not following group rules may be removed. Thank you for taking extra steps to keep this community positive and helpful! ____________________________________________

The word Isha means “that which is the basis of everything.” Nothingness is the basis of everything. If you look at the world as various reverberations, then silence is the basis of everything. If you look at the world as various forms, then the formless is the basis. If you look at the world in terms of measurements, then the limitless is the basis.                 </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Hi there, welcome to our Adult ADHD/ADD peer support group, This is a safe place for you to get and give support, where can feel safe enough to discuss ANYTHING, except Religion and Politics, without judgment. Please note that this group is for adults with add/adhd, not for children with adhd/add. ***If you are looking for a group as a parent of a non-adult child with the diagnosis, there are other more appropriate groups*** MEMBERSHIP RULES 1. NO MED SHAMING DO not judge, criticize, or shame any members for the medication they are on, that includes not comparing it to illegal drugs 2. NO Bullying of other members in ANY form This group is a safe place for all members; to discuss/chat about ANYTHING they wish to, without judgment or harassment - as long as it doesn't go against the rules. 3. Disrespecting Moderators &amp; Admin will not be accepted 4. DO NOT Post ANY Hate Speech, Politics, or Religion 5. PEOPLE INVITED by other members MUST ALSO answer the questions 6. DO NOT POST ANY Promotions or Self-promotion, Advertising of products, or services, NO links, No Research requests, OR SELLING OF ANYTHING in the group 7. GROUP PRIVACY IS PARAMOUNT - What's shared in the group stays in the group. (sharing outside will result in being banned) 8. DO NOT Block admins/mods, it will result in being removed or blocked from the group. However, if you have an issue with another member, feel free to block or report a thread to admins/Mods 9. ADHD is not fake, or curable 10. ALWAYS BE KIND – if you can’t be nice then say nothing at all 11. RESERVE JUDGMENTAL ATTITUDE Members are free to discuss ANYTHING, as long as it is within the rules, some topics can and will make you see red; DO NOT EXPRESS THAT, scroll past! Do not make judgemental comments.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 LLLI Breastfeeding Support
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to La Leche League International's Breastfeeding Support group. The purpose of this group is to provide support to individual parents in breastfeeding their own babies. **For urgent or time-sensitive questions, please contact an LLL Leader in your area.** We can't guarantee an immediate response in the group. Local Leader contact info can be found at https://www.llli.org/get-help/ JOINING THE GROUP When you request to join the group, you'll be asked to answer a few questions. Your responses will help us to process your request more quickly. **Join requests without responses to the questions will NOT be approved.** This group is meant for those who are pregnant, breastfeeding / nursing / chestfeeding, expressing milk / pumping, or otherwise nurturing their baby with human milk, at the breast / chest or desire to. RULES Once you have been added to the group, please read the "LLLI Breastfeeding Support Group Guidelines" document in the Files section before posting: https://www.facebook.com/notes/llli-breastfeeding-support/llli-breastfeeding-support-group-guidelines/1224351567740940/ We expect all group members to be familiar with the rules. If you repeatedly break the rules or mix causes, you may be removed from the group without a reminder or warning. MIXING CAUSES This group has only one purpose: To help each member meet their own feeding goals. **Do NOT join the group to promote a cause.** Even if it's a breastfeeding-related cause. Even if it's an extremely important cause. This is not an advocacy group. We're here to support each person with that one thing that they are concerned about today. PROFESSIONAL CREDENTIALS This is a parent-to-parent support group and professional advice is outside of our scope. Medical and lactation professionals are welcome to join the group, but we ask that you respond to other members as fellow parents rather than professionals. To avoid confusion, we may NOT approve membership requests where medical or lactation credentials are included in the profile name. For example, "Jane Smith IBCLC".

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Intermittent Fasting Lifestyle
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 𝗪𝗲𝗹𝗰𝗼𝗺𝗲 𝘁𝗼 𝘁𝗵𝗶𝘀 𝗳𝗿𝗶𝗲𝗻𝗱𝗹𝘆, 𝗻𝗼𝗻-𝗷𝘂𝗱𝗴𝗺𝗲𝗻𝘁𝗮𝗹 𝗴𝗿𝗼𝘂𝗽 𝗳𝗼𝗿 𝗮𝗹𝗹 𝘁𝗵𝗶𝗻𝗴𝘀 IFL! We encourage you to share your experiences, stories, tips and progress photos. Please find the following guidelines: ➊ 𝗕𝗲 𝗿𝗲𝘀𝗽𝗲𝗰𝘁𝗳𝘂𝗹. We will delete any unfriendly, aggressive, suggestive, racist, off-topic, repetitive, violent, obscene, profane, or hateful posts, links or images. ➋ 𝗧𝗵𝗶𝘀 𝗴𝗿𝗼𝘂𝗽 𝗶𝘀 𝗳𝗼𝗿 𝗜𝗻𝘁𝗲𝗿𝗺𝗶𝘁𝘁𝗲𝗻𝘁 𝗙𝗮𝘀𝘁𝗶𝗻𝗴. Short, regular fasts for health and calorie-controlling benefits. Please do not discuss fasts that are longer than 72 hours, dry fasting or the snake diet. ➌ 𝗖𝗹𝗲𝗮𝗻 𝗳𝗮𝘀𝘁𝘀 allow only unflavoured water, black coffee, black/green tea, and salt/unsweetened electrolytes. Clean fasts lead to the most optimal weight loss and health benefits, including autophagy. Dirty fasts may compromise these. ➍ 𝗡𝗼 𝗮𝗱𝘃𝗲𝗿𝘁𝗶𝘀𝗶𝗻𝗴. No products, Facebook groups, eating regimes, or any form of self-promotion whether by link, embedded text in images, or private messaging of members without their express consent. Blocking of Admin or Moderators will result in an immediate ban. Users committing multiple offences will also be blocked from the page. 𝗛𝗼𝘄 𝘁𝗼 𝘀𝘁𝗮𝗿𝘁 𝗜𝗙 𝗶𝗻 𝟰 𝗲𝗮𝘀𝘆 𝘀𝘁𝗲𝗽𝘀. 1) Stop eating. 2) Don't eat for 16 hours. You can sleep/exercise during this time. See above note on clean fasts. 3) Select an 8-hour window of time that works best with your schedule to get all your eating done. Aim for healthy options. Sweets and junk food in moderation. Eat fewer calories than you burn. You may also exercise. 4) Go back to Step 1. Welcome to the group and don't be afraid to ask more questions. We hope you all find this page to be a useful source for finding support and sharing your IF experiences. 𝗪𝗲𝗹𝗰𝗼𝗺𝗲 𝘁𝗼 𝘁𝗵𝗲 IFL 𝗹𝗶𝗳𝗲𝘀𝘁𝘆𝗹𝗲!

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 World Recreation Association of the Deaf, Inc. (WRAD)
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 WHAT IS WRAD, INC? WRAD, Inc. is representing the community of persons that are deaf or hard of hearing and all their friends and families. We have community events in the deaf and hard of hearing community that include ASL and written English in the USA . We use international signs, English, and the language of different countries when we have events or activities abroad including communication. WRAD PROGRAMS AND ACTIVITIES WRAD has four major sections, each of which provides programs, services, and activities to hearing, deaf, and hard of hearing persons. EDUCATION Our Education Section provided truthful, accurate, and complete information on aspects including ASL and English as a Second Language including written English. CHARITABLE Our Charitable Section focuses on providing FUN, ENTERTAINING, and INFORMATIVE experiences, events, programs, and services, including community lectures, holiday parties, and events, recreation and leisure activities, travel and tour opportunities, and much more, at the lowest possible cost, in order to include persons experiencing financial hardships. All of our events are held in interesting locations within the general community, to promote inclusion. RESEARCH Our Research Section is comprised of researchers from Universities, operating under established and accepted research methodologies PUBLICATIONS Our Publication Section provides information in print, and in other media, as well as reviewing and redistributing public information materials and those of other organizations and agencies. WRAD HISTORY AND ACCOMPLISHMENTS WRAD, Inc., an International NGO organization and IRS Section 501c3 Educational, Charitable, Research, and Literary nonprofit organization, began in 1985 when Founder Bruce Gross, the deaf son of deaf parents, and a Professional Educator, decided to assist the community of persons who are deaf and hard of hearing to achieve more inclusion, acceptance, and access to the great benefits offered by general society. WRAD activities, programs, and services are open to all, without discrimination. We all learn from each other. If you have an open mind and good heart, and if you celebrate diversity, and wish to learn from others who may be quite different from you, and to learn to accommodate differences in the interests of mutual understanding, come and join us!!!! We also welcome affiliates from different organizations and agencies that have an open mind and a good heart about issues on deafness. In the past, the name of our organization meant "World Recreation Association of the Deaf and Hard of Hearing," which was abbrevicated "WRAD." The WRAD organization was incorporated in 1985 under all four of the IRS categories for IRC Section 501(c)(3) nonprofit public benefit organizations. WRAD has always had four sections:Educational, Charitable, Scientific Research, and Literary Media and Publications. 
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Inspirational quotes have been one of the main reasons for the success of many people. Reading motivational and inspiring quotes on a daily basis has been reported time and again to boost a person's motivation, and help them to take action towards what they want. Overall, reading inspirational quotes on a regular basis can help a person become more successful, and lead a happier, more fulfilling life. There are literally thousands of great quotes to choose from, providing people with a never-ending supply of free motivation including our page.                 <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 1. Be kind and courteous. Negative behavior on a post or towards someone will not be tolerated. Repeat offenders will be banned. We are not here to judge, but rather to support one another. 2. Along the same lines, NO posts pertaining to sex in ANY way will be permitted. They will be deleted without warning 4. No selfies or going live (Even as an introduction.) This will result in an immediate ban. We see this kind of behavior as attention seeking, regardless of your intent. 5. We accept people of ALL religions, colors, creed, sexual orientations, and genders. Hate against anyone for ANY of these or any other reasons will NOT be tolerated. It could result in a ban, and repeat offenders will be banned. 6. No soliciting or spam. This includes, but is not limited to, advertising your company, product, trying to gain members for another group or followers for a page, soliciting without asking for money and GoFundMe. Anyone soliciting for ANY reason will be instantly banned. 7. If you laugh react to a post that is not meant to be funny, you will be banned. 8. No asking to meet in real life for any reason. 9. This group is 100% private! Taking ANYthing outside of the group will result in an instant ban! Respect EVERYONE'S privacy at ALL times! This means that you will not message any member of the group, will not message any member of their friends list or family, will not contact any type of law enforcement, or mental health professional WITHOUT the consent of the poster! Anyone caught doing so will be banned no questions asked. 10. While we accept discussion of medication and drugs, please refrain from selling, or posting photos of them. This especially goes for marijuana. Your post will be deleted. 11. If you have a complaint about a member, a post, or anything else, PLEASE talk to a moderator or member of the admin. Do NOT make a post within the group. Your post will be deleted without warning. 12. If you wish to leave the group, please do so quietly. If you make a post threatening to leave, talking about how you’re contemplating leaving, we will ban you asap. 13. No photos of minors 14. If you see something that violates a rule, please report it or contact a mod/admin. 15. If something bothers you, or triggers you, but does not break a rule, please just scroll past. If you are a repeat complainer of such things, it could result in a ban from the group, so do not come to the staff complaining of being triggered, or make a post along the same lines withing the group. 16. Do NOT block any member of the staff. We will find you, and we will ban you. 17. The staff of this group are NOT your personal mental health professionals.

Ai thấy có bài viết nào hay trên FB hay trên Web thì chia sẻ vào đây cho mọi người củng xem nhé Các chủ đề chính: * Giữ gìn sức khỏe, phòng bệnh * Bài thuốc chữa bệnh * Cách thức ăn uống tốt cho sức khỏe * Thể dục, vận động * Giữ tâm an lạc QUY ĐỊNH CỦA NHÓM 1 - Không được đăng bài quảng cáo Những bài có tính chất quảng cáo sẽ không được duyệt, trừ những trường hợp có ích chung được admin cho phép 2 - Tôn trọng lẫn nhau, không được công kích cá nhân Tranh luận góp ý được khuyến khích để học hỏi lẫn nhau, nhưng phải trên tinh thần tôn trọng lẫn nhau, không được công kích cá nhân 3 - Không bàn chuyện ngoài lề, chính trị hay nhạy cảm Nhóm tập trung vào chủ đề chăm sóc bảo vệ sức khỏe cả về thể chất lẫn tinh thần. Không bàn các chủ đề ngoài lề, nhất là chính trị hay các chủ đề nhạy cảm gây tranh cãi trái chiều 4 - Vi phạm luật có thể bị đưa ra khỏi nhóm Người vi phạm luật của nhóm có thể bị mute (không comment được) một thời gian, bị nhắc nhở hay bị đưa ra khỏi nhóm tùy theo mức độ vi phạm 
                </div>

                 ** YOU MUST ANSWER ALL THREE QUESTIONS WHEN REQUESTING TO JOIN. IF YOU DO NOT ANSWER ALL THREE QUESTIONS, YOU WILL BE DENIED. The privacy of our members is of the utmost importance and we want to make sure everyone who requests to join is a mama or mama to be. We allow joint profiles, but mamas only, please! While we love that daddies want to be involved in their baby's breastfeeding journey, we try and make this a safe space for all moms. If you are a dad trying to find support and get questions answered, please message an admin and we can direct you to different groups that will better fit your needs. If you have trouble with the questions, message an admin or our business page Milky Mamas Breastfeeding Support. ABOUT: This is a non-discriminatory breastfeeding support group without borders. Ask questions, share your struggles, and celebrate your achievements! We welcome mamas of all ages, ethnicities, and walks of life. If you need support or help, we are here for you! Everyone operates under the expectation that your child receiving all, or primarily, breastmilk is the goal. We support breastfeeding, pumping, SNS, use of donor milk, wet nursing, supplementing and solids when the time comes (6 months and no earlier). We operate with a responsive/gentle/attachment parenting philosophy. We do not allow endorsements, recommendations, or “success stories” about sleep methods that involve any form of cry it out (CIO). *NO ADVERTISING OF PRODUCTS OR SERVICES, WORK AT HOME BUSINESS OPPORTUNITIES, MLM, ETC. WE HAVE A ZERO TOLERANCE POLICY FOR THIS. Products and services can be advertised on the "Sell Yourself Sunday" post on Sundays ONLY.                 <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Visionary Mental Health
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Formerly known as 'The Shamanic View of Mental Illness', this group is designed to be a safe space for people wishing to explore indigenous and non-western approaches to mental health challenges. It also includes any areas of modern western mental health that honour and embrace a holistic focus and are not dismissive of the potential value of spiritual perspectives. Fundamental principles of Visionary Mental Health. - Non-ordinary or visionary states of consciousness have been experienced throughout human history. In many other cultures these experiences were, and are, valued and not labelled as a sickness. - The way we label our experiences influences our experiences. - A non-ordinary state of consciousness is not madness, but may lead to madness. - According to 'The Better Outcomes Hypothesis', which is a series of longitudinal studies over a 3 decade long period, developing nations not using the modern medical approach to metal health crisis have better outcomes. This group and the growing body of research around Visionary Mental Health aims to understand why this is the case.

                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 *In order to join, you must answer the required question.* This is a group for mothers of children on the autism spectrum. We are a support system where we give advice and comfort to one another. We try to maintain a positive environment and ask members to be respectful and supportive. If you don’t have anything helpful or supportive to add to a post, we ask you to not say anything. Sometimes moms just want to vent. We ask that you don’t criticize or make judgments. By requesting to join the group, you are agreeing to follow the group rules and understand that failure to respect the group rules may result in being removed from the group. We review all potential members’ profiles in order to make a decision whether to admit you to the group. If we don’t have enough information, your request will be denied. Very new profiles will not be allowed. Group posts are moderated, meaning that all posts are reviewed by the admin team before being posted to ensure compliance with our rules. We keep a close watch and remove posts and comments that break the rules. For example, we do not allow any posts or comments discussing vaccines or cures of autism or spanking or other physical punishments of our children. If you disagree with any of our rules, then this isn’t the group for you. The admin team is made up of busy mothers who all have autistic children of our own. We are all unpaid volunteers and give up our own time to keep this group a safe place for people to support one another. Disrespect of any members of the admin team will not be tolerated. Before posting we ask you to first look in the Topics section or use the group Search feature to see if your topic of interest has already been covered.

ATTENTION: We do screen ALL profiles so there is still a chance that spammers will get in even though it is a closed group. We always recommend that you NOT share personal contact info, addresses, etc on the public post and share it only via PM.. If you are seeking general Travel Support or advice please see our Network group here: https://www.facebook.com/groups/TheGypsyNurseNetwork/ Housing Listings are not allowed in this group and will be deleted. If you need housing or have housing to post, please post to our housing group here: https://www.facebook.com/groups/travelnursehousing/ Please note: ANY post that violates the following Social Media Guidelines produced by the NCSBN will be immediately deleted without notification. Repeat offenders will be removed and banned from the Gypsy Nurse group(s). Please review the guidelines here: https://www.ncsbn.org/Social_Media.pdf
                </div>
               </div>

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Sensory Processing Disorder (SPD) Support
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is comprised primarily of parents who are raising children with SPD. Adults living with SPD and therapy providers are here (and welcome) but do note that families are in the *majority* here. Sensory Planet was founded in early 2009 with a primary goal: to bring a positive, purposeful and valuable social network community to those whose lives are affected by Sensory Processing Disorder. Our group policies have been posted in the FILES section (the file name is: Group Policies January 2015.pdf). Please take a moment to read both the 2015 file and the pinned post as both inform you about how our group is moderated. There are some topics that aren't a good fit for this group, so be advised that they may be removed without discussion by an administrator: GoFundMe or any similar fundraising, Facebook Live Videos, Watch Parties, car seat safety, essential oils and vaccinations (this is not an all-inclusive list, but know that these are high trigger topics, so don't engage in them here -- they will be deleted by a moderator). There are plenty of groups on Facebook where these conversations are welcomed and engaged in regularly -- please join them if that is your area of interest. Group Owner: Carrie Fannin Assisting Moderators (and all-around generous, wonderful and supportive VOLUNTEERS!): ❤ Audrey Finnearty Meagan Johnson Day Kerri Peetz Engebrecht Lynn Wayman

                 I USE A WHEELCHAIR, Yes I Have A Life.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 .https://www.facebook.com/groups/117559551611045 I like to invite you to our wheelchair group,we are now over 11,200 members. This group is unique in ways,we don't just talk about our wheelchair and the disability,we talk about life and the things we enjoy,being music,movies,sports or some that are into wheelchair sports.the main thing is to try to get to know each other better.more like a large family.. these days I see nothing wrong with using a wheelchair, these days there sporty and lightweight plus also as the baby boomers get old your going to see more wheelchairs,scooters and etc. I check all members before they join the group, and make sure there suited for this group. I can't guarantee that some troll or predators well slip in the group Your welcome to join this group if you use a wheelchair,have a family member or close friend that uses a wc.... No spam or selling things on group also please don't talk about religion or .political things unless it's deal with disability One thing I have is a zero tolerance for arguing and calling members names or causing trouble. This group is mainly for all ages that use a wheelchair, so please no swearing or sexual talk or photo on this group.. Founded May 8,2010 If you already join Tell all your friends that use a wheelchair about this group. The number one group for wheelchair users on Facebook
